       <td style="padding:0px;">
        <div style="padding:2px;text-align:left;border-bottom:1px #aaa solid;">
         <a href="/wiki/Coproduct" title="Coproduct">
          coproduct
         </a>
        </div>
        <div style="padding:2px;text-align:center;border-bottom:1px #aaa solid;">
         coproduct over ... from ... to ... of
        </div>
        <div style="padding:2px;text-align:right;">
         <a href="/wiki/Category_theory" title="Category theory">
          category theory
         </a>
        </div>
       </td>
       <td>
        A general construction which subsumes the
        <a href="/wiki/Disjoint_union" title="Disjoint union">
         disjoint union of sets
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Disjoint_union_(topology)" title="Disjoint union (topology)">
         of topological spaces
        </a>
        , the
        <a href="/wiki/Free_product" title="Free product">
         free product of groups
        </a>
        , and the
        <a href="/wiki/Direct_sum" title="Direct sum">
         direct sum
        </a>
        of modules and vector spaces. The coproduct of a family of objects is essentially the "least specific" object to which each object in the family admits a
        <a href="/wiki/Morphism" title="Morphism">
         morphism
        </a>
        .
       </td>

       </td>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Variations">
       Variations
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_mathematical_symbols&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Variations">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      In mathematics written in
      <a href="/wiki/Arabic_language" title="Arabic language">
       Arabic
      </a>
      , some symbols may be reversed to make right-to-left writing and reading easier.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">
       <a href="#cite_note-13">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        13
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>

           OCLC
          </a>
          <a class="external text" href="//www.worldcat.org/oclc/43641333" rel="nofollow">
           43641333
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+mathematical+symbols&amp;rft.au=Chuang%2C+Isaac+L&amp;rft.aufirst=Michael+A&amp;rft.aulast=Nielsen&amp;rft.au=Nielsen%2C+Michael+A&amp;rft.btitle=Quantum+Computation+and+Quantum+Information&amp;rft.date=2000&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft_id=info%3Aoclcnum%2F43641333&amp;rft.isbn=0-521-63503-9&amp;rft.pages=71-72&amp;rft.place=New+York&amp;rft.pub=Cambridge+University+Press&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook">
          <span style="display:none;">
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </li>
       <li id="cite_note-13">
        <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
         <b>
          <a href="#cite_ref-13">
           ^
          </a>
         </b>
        </span>
        <span class="reference-text">
         M. Benatia, A. Lazrik, and K. Sami, "
         <a class="external text" href="http://www.ucam.ac.ma/fssm/rydarab/doc/expose/unicodeme.pdf" rel="nofollow">
          Arabic mathematical symbols in Unicode
         </a>
         ", 27th Internationalization and Unicode Conference, 2005.
        </span>
       </li>
      </ol>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="External_links">
       External links
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_mathematical_symbols&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: External links">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://krestavilis.com/math.php" rel="nofollow">
        The complete set of mathematics Unicode characters
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://jeff560.tripod.com/mathsym.html" rel="nofollow">
        Jeff Miller:
        <i>
         Earliest Uses of Various Mathematical Symbols
        </i>
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.numericana.com/answer/symbol.htm" rel="nofollow">
        Numericana:
        <i>
         Scientific Symbols and Icons
        </i>
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://us.metamath.org/symbols/symbols.html" rel="nofollow">
        GIF and PNG Images for Math Symbols
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://tlt.psu.edu/suggestions/international/bylanguage/math.html#browsers" rel="nofollow">
        Mathematical Symbols in Unicode
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.alanwood.net/demos/symbol.html" rel="nofollow">
        Using Greek and special characters from Symbol font in HTML
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://mathsymbols.net/" rel="nofollow">
        Unicode Math Symbols
       </a>
       - a quick form for using unicode math symbols.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://detexify.kirelabs.org/classify.html" rel="nofollow">
        DeTeXify handwritten symbol recognition
       </a>
        doodle a symbol in the box, and the program will tell you what its name is
      </li>
     </ul>
     <p>
      Some Unicode charts of mathematical operators:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.unicode.org/charts/#symbols" rel="nofollow">
        Index of Unicode symbols
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.unicode.org/charts/PDF/U2100.pdf" rel="nofollow">
        Range 2100214F: Unicode Letterlike Symbols
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.unicode.org/charts/PDF/U2190.pdf" rel="nofollow">
        Range 219021FF: Unicode Arrows
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.unicode.org/charts/PDF/U2200.pdf" rel="nofollow">
        Range 220022FF: Unicode Mathematical Operators
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.unicode.org/charts/PDF/U27C0.pdf" rel="nofollow">
        Range 27C027EF: Unicode Miscellaneous Mathematical SymbolsA
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.unicode.org/charts/PDF/U2980.pdf" rel="nofollow">
        Range 298029FF: Unicode Miscellaneous Mathematical SymbolsB
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.unicode.org/charts/PDF/U2A00.pdf" rel="nofollow">
        Range 2A002AFF: Unicode Supplementary Mathematical Operators
       </a>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <p>
      Some Unicode cross-references:
     </p>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.artofproblemsolving.com/Wiki/index.php/LaTeX:Symbols" rel="nofollow">
        Short list of commonly used LaTeX symbols
       </a>
       and
       <a class="external text" href="http://mirrors.med.harvard.edu/ctan/info/symbols/comprehensive/" rel="nofollow">
        Comprehensive LaTeX Symbol List
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.robinlionheart.com/stds/html4/entities-mathml" rel="nofollow">
        MathML Characters
       </a>
       - sorts out Unicode, HTML and MathML/TeX names on one page
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.w3.org/TR/REC-MathML/chap6/bycodes.html" rel="nofollow">
        Unicode values and MathML names
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://svn.ghostscript.com/ghostscript/branches/gs-db/Resource/Decoding/Unicode" rel="nofollow">
        Unicode values and Postscript names
       </a>
       from the source code for
       <a href="/wiki/Ghostscript" title="Ghostscript">
        Ghostscript
       </a>
      </li>
     </ul>
